<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0 0pt 1in; text-indent: -1in">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0"><span style="font-family: Times New Roman, Times, Serif">(b)&#160;As
reported in 3M Company&#8217;s press release dated Januray 28, 2020, Julie L. Bushman, executive vice president, international
operations, has</span> announced her intention to retire, effective April 1, 2020. Prior to her current role, Ms. Bushman led 3M&#8217;s
Safety and Graphics business group, business transformation and IT and was on the original leadership team that implemented Lean
Six Sigma at 3M.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#8220;Throughout her 36 years at 3M, Julie has been an exceptional
leader and created tremendous value for our company and shareholders,&#8221; Mike Roman, 3M chairman and chief executive officer,
said. &#8220;Julie&#8217;s leadership has been invaluable throughout her time leading our international team, including playing
a critical role in our transformation journey.&#8221;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#8220;Over the last year, her leadership has been key as we
have worked closely together to design and roll out our new operating model, and ensure a smooth transition,&#8221; Roman continued.
&#8220;I thank Julie for her many years of service and contributions, and wish her all the best into the future.&#8221;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0pt 0">&#160;&#160;</p>
